The following tables compare general and technical features of a number of [[email client]] programs. Please see the individual products' articles for further information.

==Features==

Information on what features each of the clients support.

===General features===

For all of these clients, the concept of "HTML support" does not mean that they can process the full range of HTML that a web browser can handle. Almost all email readers limit HTML features, either for security reasons, or because of the nature of the interface. CSS and JavaScript can be especially problematic. A number of articles describe these limitations per-email-client; see [http://www.campaignmonitor.com/blog/archives/2005/11/html_email_desi.html 1], [http://www.sitepoint.com/article/code-html-email-newsletters 2], [http://alistapart.com/articles/cssemail/ 3], and [http://www.campaignmonitor.com/blog/archives/2006/03/a_guide_to_css_1.html 4]

! rowspan="2" | [[UTF-8]] support
! rowspan="2" | Image blocking
! colspan="2" | [[email spam|Junk]] filtering
! rowspan="2" | [[Phishing]] filtering
! rowspan="2" | Thread view
! rowspan="2" | Conversation view
! colspan="2" | [[Pretty Good Privacy|PGP]] support
! colspan="4" | [[S/MIME]] support
|-class="sortbottom"
! local
! server- side
! inline
! PGP/MIME or OpenPGP
! protocol
! [[OCSP]]
! [[Certificate revocation list|CRL]]
! certificates on tokens, smartcards support
|}
<ref name="TBCRL" group="Note">The Bat! supports two modes of S/MIME: Internal Implementation and via [[Microsoft Crypto API]]. CRLs and OCSP are only supported in the latter mode. Internal implementation only supports Aladdin eToken Pro or Rainbow iKey1000 tokens and can import certificates (from PKCS#12/PFX format) which were created outside The Bat!. CryptoAPI supports any kind of tokens and smart cards which have a corresponding [[Cryptographic Service Provider]] installed.</ref>

==Internationalization==
[[The Bat!]] supports [[Email Address Internationalization]] (EAI).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template noprint Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i>[[WP:NOTRS|<span title="This claim needs references to better sources. (October 2013)">better&nbsp;source&nbsp;needed</span>]]</i>&#93;</sup><sup class="noprint selfreference">&#91;''[[#International email|discuss]]''&#93;</sup>

As of April, 2014, there are no email clients that support SMTPUTF8.
